Get task from database\n        task = db_session.query(Task).filter(Task.id == task_id).first()\n        if not task:\n            logger.error(f"Task {task_id} not found")\n            return\n        \n        # Update task status\n        task.status = "running"\n        task.started_at = datetime.utcnow()\n        db_session.commit()\n        \n        logger.info(f"Starting task execution: {task.title} (ID: {task_id})")\n        \n        # Create orchestrator\n        orchestrator = MultiAgentOrchestrator()\n        \n        # Execute task based on type\n        result = None\n        if task.task_type == "research":\n            agent = ResearcherAgent()\n            query = task.parameters.get("query", task.description)\n            result = await agent.research(query)\n            \n        elif task.task_type == "code":\n            agent = CoderAgent()\n            language = task.parameters.get("language", "python")\n            description = task.parameters.get("description", task.description)\n            result = await agent.generate_code(description, language)\n            \n        elif task.task_type == "website":\n            # Use orchestrator for complex website creation\n            result = await orchestrator.execute_task(\n                task_type="website",\n                description=task.description,\n                parameters=task.parameters\n            )\n            \n        elif task.task_type == "analysis":\n            agent = AnalystAgent()\n            data = task.parameters.get("data", [])\n            analysis_type = task.parameters.get("analysis_type", "descriptive")\n            result = await agent.analyze(data, analysis_type)\n            \n        elif task.task_type == "debug":\n            agent = DebuggerAgent()\n            error_message = task.parameters.get("error_message", "")\n            code = task.parameters.get("code", "")\n            result = await agent.debug(error_message, code)\n            \n        elif task.task_type == "documentation":\n            agent = WriterAgent()\n            doc_type = task.parameters.get("doc_type", "readme")\n            content = task.parameters.get("content", {})\n            result = await agent.write_documentation(doc_type, content)\n        \n        else:\n            # Use orchestrator for complex tasks\n            result = await orchestrator.execute_task(\n                task_type=task.task_type,\n                description=task.description,\n                parameters=task.parameters\n            )\n        \n        # Update task with result\n        task.status = "completed"\n        task.progress = 100\n        task.result = result\n        task.completed_at = datetime.utcnow()\n        db_session.commit()\n        \n        logger.info(f"Task completed successfully: {task.title} (ID: {task_id})")\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f"Task execution failed: {str(e)}")\n        \n        # Update task with error\n        task = db_session.query(Task).filter(Task.id == task_id).first()\n        if task:\n            task.status = "failed"\n            task.error = str(e)\n            task.completed_at = datetime.utcnow()\n            db_session.commit()\n\n@router.post("/", response_model=TaskResponse, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\nasync def create_task(\n    task_data: TaskCreate,\n    background_tasks: BackgroundTasks,\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user),\n    db: Session = Depends(get_db)\n):\n    """\n    Create a new task\n    \n    - **title**: Task title\n    - **description**: Detailed task description\n    - **task_type**: Type of task (research, code, website, analysis, debug, documentation)\n    - **parameters**: Additional parameters for the task\n    - **template_id**: Optional template to use\n    """\n    # Validate task type\n    valid_types = ["research", "code", "website", "analysis", "debug", "documentation", "custom"]\n    if task_data.task_type not in valid_types:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,\n            detail=f"Invalid task type. Must be one of: {\', \'.join(valid_types)}"\n        )\n    \n    # If template_id provided, load template\n    if task_data.template_id:\n        template = db.query(Template).filter(Template.id ==     )\n        # Merge template parameters with provided parameters\n        task_data.parameters = {**template.parameters, **task_data.parameters}\n    \n    # Create task\n    task = Task(\n status="pending",\n        progress=0\n    )\n    \n    db.add(task)\n    db.commit()\n    db.refresh(task)\n    \n    logger.info(f"Task created: {task.title} (ID: {task.id}) by user {current_user.email}")\n    \n    # Execute task in background\n    background_tasks.add_task(execute_task_background, task.id, db)\n    \n    return TaskResponse(\n        id=task.id,\n error=task.error,\n        created_at=task.created_at.isoformat(),\n        started_at=task.started_at.isoformat() if task.started_at else None,\n        completed_at=task.completed_at.isoformat() if task.completed_at else None\n    )\n\n@router.get("/", response_model=List[TaskResponse])\nasync def list_tasks(\n    skip: int = 0,\n    limit: int = 50,\n    status: Optional[str] = None,\n Documents\n    ".txt", ".md", ".pdf", ".doc", ".docx",\n    # Code\n    ".py", ".js", ".ts", ".java", ".go", ".rs", ".c", ".cpp", ".rb", ".php",\n    # Data\n    ".json", ".csv", ".xml", ".yaml", ".yml",\n    # Create vercel.json if not exists\n        vercel_config = source_path / "vercel.json"\n        if not vercel_config.exists():\n            with open(vercel_config, "w") as f:\n                json.dump({\n                    "version": 2,\n                    "name": name,\n                    "builds": [\n                        {"src": "**/*.html", "use": "@vercel/static"}\n                    ]\n                }, f)\n        \n        # Deploy using Vercel CLI\n        cmd = [\n            "vercel",\n            "--token", vercel_token,\n            "--prod",\n            "--yes",\n            str(source_path)\n        ]\n        \n        result = subprocess.run(\n            cmd,\n            capture_output=True,\n            text=True,\n            timeout=300\n        )\n        \n        if result.returncode != 0:\n            raise Exception(f"Vercel deployment failed: {result.stderr}")\n        \n        # Extract URL from output\n        url = result.stdout.strip().split("\\n")[-1]\n        \n        return {\n            "status": "deployed",\n            "url": url,\n            "deployed_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()\n        }\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f"Vercel deployment error: {e}")\n        return {\n            "status": "failed",\n            "error": str(e)\n        }\n\nasync def deploy_to_netlify(\n    deployment_id: str,\n    name: str,\n    source_path: Path,\n    config: dict\n) -> dict:\n    """Deploy to Netlify"""\n    try:\n        netlify_token = config.get("netlify_token")\n        if not netlify_token:\n            raise ValueError("Netlify token not provided")\n        \n        # Deploy using Netlify CLI\n        cmd = [\n            "netlify",\n            "deploy",\n            "--prod",\n            "--auth", netlify_token,\n            "--dir", str(source_path),\n            "--site", name\n        ]\n        \n        result = subprocess.run(\n            cmd,\n            capture_output=True,\n            text=True,\n            timeout=300\n        )\n        \n        if result.returncode != 0:\n            raise Exception(f"Netlify deployment failed: {result.stderr}")\n        \n        # Extract URL from output\n        lines = result.stdout.strip().split("\\n")\n        url = None\n        for line in lines:\n            if "Website URL:" in line:\n                url = line.split("Website URL:")[-1].strip()\n                break\n        \n        return {\n            "status": "deployed",\n            "url": url or f"https://{name}.netlify.app",\n            "deployed_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()\n        }\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f"Netlify deployment error: {e}")\n        return {\n            "status": "failed",\n            "error": str(e)\n        }\n\nasync def deploy_to_github_pages(\n    deployment_id: str,\n    name: str,\n    source_path: Path,\n    config: dict\n) -> dict:\n    """Deploy to GitHub Pages"""\n    try:\n        github_token = config.get("github_token")\n        repo = config.get("github_repo")\n        \n        if not github_token or not repo:\n            raise ValueError("GitHub token and repo required")\n        \n        # Initialize git repo if not exists\n        git_dir = source_path / ".git"\n        if not git_dir.exists():\n            subprocess.run(["git", "init"], cwd=source_path, check=True)\n            subprocess.run(\n                ["git", "remote", "add", "origin", f"https://{github_token}@github.com/{repo}.git"],\n                cwd=source_path,\n                check=True\n            )\n        \n        # Commit and push\n        subprocess.run(["git", "add", "."], cwd=source_path, check=True)\n        subprocess.run(\n            ["git", "commit", "-m", f"Deploy {deployment_id}"],\n            cwd=source_path,\n            check=True\n        )\n        subprocess.run(\n            ["git", "push", "-f", "origin", "main:gh-pages"],\n            cwd=source_path,\n            check=True\n        )\n        \n        # Extract username and repo name\n        username = repo.split("/")[0]\n        repo_name = repo.split("/")[1]\n        \n        return {\n            "status": "deployed",\n            "url": f"https://{username}.github.io/{repo_name}",\n            "deployed_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()\n        }\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f"GitHub Pages deployment error: {e}")\n        return {\n            "status": "failed",\n            "error": str(e)\n        }\n\nasync def deploy_to_s3(\n    deployment_id: str,\n    name: str,\n    source_path: Path,\n    config: dict\n) -> dict:\n    """Deploy to AWS S3"""\n    try:\n        import boto3\n        \n        aws_access_key = config.get("aws_access_key")\n        aws_secret_key = config.get("aws_secret_key")\n        aws_region = config.get("aws_region", "us-east-1")\n        bucket_name = config.get("bucket_name", name)\n        \n        if not aws_access_key or not aws_secret_key:\n            raise ValueError("AWS credentials required")\n        \n        # Create S3 client\n        s3 = boto3.client(\n            \'s3\',\n            aws_access_key_id=aws_access_key,\n            aws_secret_access_key=aws_secret_key,\n            region_name=aws_region\n        )\n        \n        # Create bucket if not exists\n        try:\n            s3.create_bucket(Bucket=bucket_name)\n            \n            # Enable static website hosting\n            s3.put_bucket_website(\n                Bucket=bucket_name,\n                WebsiteConfiguration={\n                    \'IndexDocument\': {\'Suffix\': \'index.html\'},\n                    \'ErrorDocument\': {\'Key\': \'error.html\'}\n                }\n            )\n            \n            # Make bucket public\n            s3.put_bucket_policy(\n                Bucket=bucket_name,\n                Policy=json.dumps({\n                    "Version": "2012-10-17",\n                    "Statement": [{\n                        "Sid": "PublicReadGetObject",\n                        "Effect": "Allow",\n                        "Principal": "*",\n                        "Action": "s3:GetObject",\n                        "Resource": f"arn:aws:s3:::{bucket_name}/*"\n                    }]\n                })\n            )\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.warning(f"Bucket creation warning: {e}")\n        \n        # Upload files\n        for file_path in source_path.rglob("*"):\n            if file_path.is_file():\n                relative_path = file_path.relative_to(source_path)\n                s3.upload_file(\n                    str(file_path),\n                    bucket_name,\n                    str(relative_path),\n                    ExtraArgs={\'ContentType\': \'text/html\' if file_path.suffix == \'.html\' else \'application/octet-stream\'}\n                )\n        \n        url = f"http://{bucket_name}.s3-website-{aws_region}.amazonaws.com"\n        \n        return {\n            "status": "deployed",\n            "url": url,\n            "deployed_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()\n        }\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f"S3 deployment error: {e}")\n        return {\n            "status": "failed",\n            "error": str(e)\n        }\n\n@router.post("/", response_model=DeploymentResponse, status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)\nasync def create_deployment(\n    deployment_data: DeploymentCreate,\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)\n):\n    """\n    Create a new deployment\n    \n    - **name**: Deployment name\n    - **platform**: Target platform (vercel, netlify, github-pages, s3)\n    - **source_path**: Path to source files (relative to user\'s upload directory)\n    - **config**: Platform-specific configuration\n    """\n    # Validate platform\n    valid_platforms = ["vercel", "netlify", "github-pages", "s3"]\n    if deployment_data.platform not in valid_platforms:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,\n            detail=f"Invalid platform. Must be one of: {\', \'.join(valid_platforms)}"\n        )\n    \n    # Get source path\n    source_path = Path("uploads") / str(current_user.id) / deployment_data.source_path\n    if not source_path.exists():\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,\n            detail="Source path not found"\n        )\n    \n    # Generate deployment ID\n    deployment_id = generate_deployment_id()\n    \n    # Create deployment record\n    deployment = {\n        "id": deployment_id,\n        "user_id": current_user.id,\n        "name": deployment_data.name,\n        "platform": deployment_data.platform,\n        "source_path": str(source_path),\n        "status": "pending",\n        "created_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),\n        "deployed_at": None,\n        "url": None,\n        "error": None\n    }\n    \n    deployments_db[deployment_id] = deployment\n    \n    logger.info(f"Deployment created: {deployment_id} by user {current_user.email}")\n    \n    # Deploy based on platform\n    try:\n        if deployment_data.platform == "vercel":\n            result = await deploy_to_vercel(\n                deployment_id,\n                deployment_data.name,\n                source_path,\n                deployment_data.config\n            )\n        elif deployment_data.platform == "netlify":\n            result = await deploy_to_netlify(\n                deployment_id,\n                deployment_data.name,\n                source_path,\n                deployment_data.config\n            )\n        elif deployment_data.platform == "github-pages":\n            result = await deploy_to_github_pages(\n                deployment_id,\n                deployment_data.name,\n                source_path,\n                deployment_data.config\n            )\n        elif deployment_data.platform == "s3":\n            result = await deploy_to_s3(\n                deployment_id,\n                deployment_data.name,\n                source_path,\n                deployment_data.config\n            )\n        \n        # Update deployment record\n        deployment.update(result)\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f"Deployment error: {e}")\n        deployment["status"] = "failed"\n        deployment["error"] = str(e)\n    \n    return DeploymentResponse(**deployment)\n\n@router.get("/", response_model=List[DeploymentResponse])\nasync def list_deployments(\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)\n):\n    """List all deployments for current user"""\n    user_deployments = [\n        DeploymentResponse(**d)\n        for d in deployments_db.values()\n        if d["user_id"] == current_user.id\n    ]\n    \n    # Sort by created_at (newest first)\n    user_deployments.sort(key=lambda x: x.created_at, reverse=True)\n    \n    return user_deployments\n\n@router.get("/{deployment_id}", response_model=DeploymentResponse)\nasync def get_deployment(\n    deployment_id: str,\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)\n):\n    """Get deployment details"""\n    deployment = deployments_db.get(deployment_id)\n    \n    if not deployment:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,\n            detail="Deployment not found"\n        )\n    \n    if deployment["user_id"] != current_user.id:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN,\n            detail="You don\'t have permission to access this deployment"\n        )\n    \n    return DeploymentResponse(**deployment)\n\n@router.delete("/{deployment_id}", status_code=status.HTTP_204_NO_CONTENT)\nasync def delete_deployment(\n    deployment_id: str,\n    current_user: User = Depends(get_current_user)\n):\n    """Delete a deployment record"""\n    deployment = deployments_db.get(deployment_id)\n    \n    if not deployment:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,\n            detail="Deployment not found"\n        )\n    \n    if deployment["user_id"] != current_user.id:\n        raise HTTPException(\n            status_code=status.HTTP_403_FORBIDDEN,\n            detail="You don\'t have permission to delete this deployment"\n        )\n    \n    del deployments_db[deployment_id]\n    \n    logger.info(f"Deployment deleted: {deployment_id}")\n    \n    return None\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

**Use Strong Secret Key**: Generate a secure SECRET_KEY (min 32 characters)\n3. **Enable HTTPS**: Use reverse proxy (nginx/traefik) with SSL certificates\n4. **Rotate API Keys**: Regularly rotate API keys and tokens\n5. **Monitor Audit Logs**: Review audit logs for suspicious activity\n6. **Limit CORS Origins**: Only allow trusted frontend domains\n7. **Use Environment Variables**: Never commit secrets to version control\n\n##  Production Deployment\n\n### Using Docker Compose\n\n1. **Update environment variables**\n```bash\n# Set production values in **Enable SSL/TLS**\n```bash\n# Use nginx or traefik as reverse proxy\n# Configure SSL certificates (Let\'s Encrypt)\n```\n\n4. **Scale services**\n```bash\ndocker-compose up -d --scale logs -f\n```\n\n### Stop Services\n```bash\n./stop.sh\n```\n\n### Restart Services\n```bash\ndocker-compose restart\n```\n\n### Check Service Status\n```bash\ndocker-compose ps\n```\n\n## Next Vercel, Netlify, or S3\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Port Already in Use\n```bash\n# Change ports in docker-compose.yml\n# Or stop the conflicting service\nlsof -i :8000\nkill -9 <PID>\n```\n\n### Database Connection Error\n```bash\n# Restart PostgreSQL\ndocker-compose restart postgres\n```\n\n### Permission Denied (Docker Socket)\n```bash\n# Add user to docker group\nsudo usermod -aG docker $USER\n# Logout and login again\n```\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Add AI Provider API Keys\n\nEdit `.env` Ninja VS Code Extension\n * Main extension entry point\n */\nimport * as vscode from \'vscode\';\nimport { ApiClient } from \'./api/client\';\nimport { TerminalManager } from \'./terminal/manager\';\nimport { TasksProvider } from \'./providers/tasksProvider\';\nimport { AgentsProvider } from \'./providers/agentsProvider\';\nimport { FilesProvider } from \'./providers/filesProvider\';\nimport { AuthManager } from \'./auth/manager\';\n\nlet apiClient: ApiClient;\nlet terminalManager: TerminalManager;\nlet authManager: AuthManager;\n\nexport async function activate(context: vscode.ExtensionContext) {\n    console.log(\'iTechSmart Ninja extension is now active!\');\n\n    // Initialize managers\n    authManager = new AuthManager(context);\n    apiClient = new ApiClient(authManager);\n    terminalManager = new TerminalManager(apiClient, context);\n\n    // Register tree data providers\n    const tasksProvider = new TasksProvider(apiClient);\n    const agentsProvider = new AgentsProvider(apiClient);\n    const filesProvider = new FilesProvider(apiClient);\n\n    vscode.window.registerTreeDataProvider(\'itechsmart.tasksView\', tasksProvider);\n    vscode.window.registerTreeDataProvider(\'itechsmart.agentsView\', agentsProvider);\n    vscode.window.registerTreeDataProvider(\'itechsmart.filesView\', filesProvider);\n\n    // Register commands\n    context.subscriptions.push(\n        // Terminal commands\n        vscode.commands.registerCommand(\'itechsmart.openTerminal\', () => {\n            terminalManager.openTerminal();\n        }),\n\n        // Authentication commands\n        vscode.commands.registerCommand(\'itechsmart.login\', async () => {\n            await authManager.login();\n            tasksProvider.refresh();\n            agentsProvider.refresh();\n            filesProvider.refresh();\n        }),\n\n        vscode.commands.registerCommand(\'itechsmart.logout\', async () => {\n            await authManager.logout();\n            tasksProvider.refresh();\n            agentsProvider.refresh();\n            filesProvider.refresh();\n        }),\n\n        // Code generation commands\n        vscode.commands.registerCommand(\'itechsmart.generateCode\', async () => {\n            const description = await vscode.window.showInputBox({\n                prompt: \'Describe what code you want to generate\',\n                placeHolder: \'e.g., Create a REST API endpoint for user authentication\'\n            });\n\n            if (description) {\n                await generateCode(description);\n            }\n        }),\n\n        // Code explanation\n        vscode.commands.registerCommand(\'itechsmart.explainCode\', async () => {\n            const editor = vscode.window.activeTextEditor;\n            if (!editor) {\n                vscode.window.showErrorMessage(\'No active editor\');\n                return;\n            }\n\n            const selection = editor.document.getText(editor.selection);\n            if (!selection) {\n                vscode.window.showErrorMessage(\'No code selected\');\n                return;\n            }\n\n            await explainCode(selection);\n        }),\n\n        // Code refactoring\n        vscode.commands.registerCommand(\'itechsmart.refactorCode\', async () => {\n            const editor = vscode.window.activeTextEditor;\n            if (!editor) {\n                vscode.window.showErrorMessage(\'No active editor\');\n                return;\n            }\n\n            const selection = editor.document.getText(editor.selection);\n            if (!selection) {\n                vscode.window.showErrorMessage(\'No code selected\');\n                return;\n            }\n\n            await refactorCode(selection, editor);\n        }),\n\n        // Code debugging\n        vscode.commands.registerCommand(\'itechsmart.debugCode\', async () => {\n            const editor = vscode.window.activeTextEditor;\n            if (!editor) {\n                vscode.window.showErrorMessage(\'No active editor\');\n                return;\n            }\n\n            const selection = editor.document.getText(editor.selection);\n            if (!selection) {\n                vscode.window.showErrorMessage(\'No code selected\');\n                return;\n            }\n\n            await debugCode(selection);\n        }),\n\n        // Task management\n        vscode.commands.registerCommand(\'itechsmart.createTask\', async () => {\n            await createTask();\n            tasksProvider.refresh();\n        }),\n\n        vscode.commands.registerCommand(\'itechsmart.viewTasks\', () => {\n            vscode.commands.executeCommand(\'workbench.view.extension.itechsmart-sidebar\');\n        }),\n\n        vscode.commands.registerCommand(\'itechsmart.refreshTasks\', () => {\n            tasksProvider.refresh();\n        }),\n\n        vscode.commands.registerCommand(\'itechsmart.cancelTask\', async (taskId: number) => {\n            await apiClient.cancelTask(taskId);\n            tasksProvider.refresh();\n        }),\n\n        vscode.commands.registerCommand(\'itechsmart.viewTaskDetails\', async (taskId: number) => {\n            await viewTaskDetails(taskId);\n        })\n    );\n\n    // Show welcome message\n    if (!authManager.isAuthenticated()) {\n        const result = await vscode.window.showInformationMessage(\n            \'Welcome to iTechSmart Ninja! Please login to get started.\',\n            \'Login\',\n            \'Later\'\n        );\n\n        if (result === \'Login\') {\n            await authManager.login();\n        }\n    } else {\n        vscode.window.showInformationMessage(\'iTechSmart Ninja is ready!\');\n    }\n\n    // Auto-refresh tasks every 30 seconds\n    setInterval(() => {\n        if (authManager.isAuthenticated()) {\n            tasksProvider.refresh();\n        }\n    }, 30000);\n}\n\nasync function generateCode(description: string) {\n    const editor = vscode.window.activeTextEditor;\n    const language = editor?.document.languageId || \'python\';\n\n    await vscode.window.withProgress({\n        location: vscode.ProgressLocation.Notification,\n        title: \'Generating code...\',\n        cancellable: false\n    }, async (progress) => {\n        try {\n            const task = await apiClient.createTask({\n                title: \'Code Generation\',\n                description: description,\n                task_type: \'code\',\n                parameters: {\n                    language: language,\n                    description: description\n                }\n            });\n\n            // Wait for task completion\n            const result = await waitForTaskCompletion(task.id, progress);\n\n            if (result && result.code) {\n                // Insert code at cursor position\n                if (editor) {\n                    editor.edit(editBuilder => {\n                        editBuilder.insert(editor.selection.active, result.code);\n                    });\n                    vscode.window.showInformationMessage(\'Code generated successfully!\');\n                } else {\n                    // Create new file\n                    const doc = await vscode.workspace.openTextDocument({\n                        content: result.code,\n                        language: language\n                    });\n                    await show tasks\n            try {\n                const tasks = await this.apiClient.getTasks({ limit: 20 });\n                return tasks.map(task => new TaskItem(task));\n            } catch (error) {\n                return [];\n            }\n        }\n        return [];\n    }\n}\n\nclass TaskItem extends vscode.TreeItem {\n    constructor(public readonly task: Task) {\n        super(task.title, vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.None);\n\n        this.description = `${task.status} (${task.progress}%)`;\n        this.tooltip = `${task.description}\\nType: ${task.task_type}\\nCreated: ${new Date(task.created_at).toLocaleString()}`;\n\n        // Set icon based on status\n        if (task.status === \'completed\') {\n            this.iconPath = new vscode.ThemeIcon(\'check\', new vscode.ThemeColor(\'testing.iconPassed\'));\n        } else if (task.status === \'failed\') {\n            this.iconPath = new vscode.ThemeIcon(\'error\', new vscode.ThemeColor(\'testing.iconFailed\'));\n        } else if (task.status === \'running\') {\n            this.iconPath = new vscode.ThemeIcon(\'sync~spin\', new vscode.ThemeColor(\'testing.iconQueued\'));\n        } else {\n            this.iconPath = new vscode.ThemeIcon(\'circle-outline\');\n        }\n\n        // Add context menu\n        this.contextValue = \'task\';\n\n        // Make clickable\n        this.command = {\n            command: \'itechsmart.viewTaskDetails\',\n            title: \'View Task Details\',\n            arguments: [task.id]\n        };\n    }\n}\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

show agents\n            try {\n                const agents = await this.apiClient.getAgents();\n                return agents.map(agent => new AgentItem(agent));\n            } catch (error) {\n                return [];\n            }\n        }\n        return [];\n    }\n}\n\nclass AgentItem extends vscode.TreeItem {\n    constructor(public readonly agent: Agent) {\n        super(agent.name, vscode.TreeItemCollapsibleState.None);\n\n        this.description = agent.type;\n        this.tooltip = `${agent.description}\\n\\nCapabilities:\\n${agent.capabilities.join(\'\\n\')}`;\n\n        // Set icon based on agent type\n        const iconMap: { [key: string]: string } = {\n            \'researcher\': \'search\',\n            \'coder\': \'code\',\n            \'writer\': \'edit\',\n            \'analyst\': \'graph\',\n            \'debugger\': \'bug\'\n        };\n\n        this.iconPath = new vscode.ThemeIcon(iconMap[agent.type] || \'robot\');\n\n        this.contextValue = \'agent\';\n    }\n}\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

Generate code from description\n- `research <query>` - Research a topic\n- `analyze <data>` - Analyze data\n- `debug <code>` - Debug code\n- `explain <code>` - Explain code\n\n### Task Management\n- `tasks` - List all tasks\n- `task <id>` - View task details\n\n### Information\n- `agents` - List available AI agents\n- `files` - List uploaded files\n- `status` - Show system status\n- `whoami` - Show current user\n\n### Terminal\n- `help` - Show help message\n- `clear` - Clear terminal\n\n## Keyboard Shortcuts\n\n- `Ctrl+Shift+I` - Open AI Terminal\n- `Ctrl+Shift+G` - Generate Code\n- `/` - Navigate command history\n- `Ctrl+L` - Clear terminal\n- `Ctrl+C` - Cancel current operation\n\n## Context Menu Commands\n\nRight-click on selected code:\n- **Explain Code** - Get detailed explanation\n- **Refactor Code** - Improve code quality\n- **Debug Code** - Find and fix errors\n\n## Sidebar Views\n\n### Tasks View\n- See all your tasks\n- Click to view details\n- Real-time status updates\n\n### Agents View\n- Browse available AI agents\n- View capabilities\n- See example tasks\n\n### Files View\n- View uploaded files\n- File size and type\n- Upload date\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Settings\n- `itechsmart.apiUrl` - Backend API URL (default: `http://localhost:8000`)\n- `itechsmart.apiKey` - API key (optional)\n- `itechsmart.defaultAgent` - Default AI agent (default: `coder`)\n- `itechsmart.autoSave` - Auto-save generated code (default: `true`)\n- `itechsmart.showNotifications` - Show task notifications (default: `true`)\n\n### Example settings.json\n```json\n{\n  "itechsmart.apiUrl": "http://localhost:8000",\n  "itechsmart.defaultAgent": "coder",\n  "itechsmart.autoSave": true,\n  "itechsmart.showNotifications": true\n}\n```\n\n## Usage Examples\n\n### Generate Code\n1. Select code\n2. Right-click  "iTechSmart: Explain Code"\n3. View detailed explanation in new panel\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Cannot connect to backend\n- Verify backend is running: `curl http://localhost:8000/health`\n- Check `itechsmart.apiUrl` setting\n- Ensure no firewall blocking\n\n### Authentication failed\n- Verify credentials\n- Check backend logs\n- Try re-login: `Ctrl+Shift+P`  "iTechSmart: Login"\n\n### Terminal not responding\n- Close and reopen terminal\n- Check backend status\n- Restart VS Code\n\n### Commands not working\n- Ensure you\'re logged in\n- Check API connection\n- View Output panel for errors\n\n## Development\n\n### Build from Source\n```bash\n# Install dependencies\nnpm install\n\n# Compile TypeScript\nnpm run compile\n\n# Watch mode\nnpm run watch\n\n# Package extension\nnpm run package\n```\n\n### Run Tests\n```bash\nnpm test\n```\n\n### Debug Extension\n1.
